 Spiritual knowledge is not necessarily exempt from tax
 maharashtra main jiesti court ne faisla diya he ki ab dharmik granth, dharmik magazine or dividi ke saath-saath dharmashala or lungar jiesti ke daayre main honge
 The court argues that the sale of these goods is a business and cannot be exempted from tax by considering them as bailouts
 maharashtra kii court ke paas tex sambandhi yah maamla shrimad rajchandra aadhyatmik satsang sadhana kendra ke khilaaf aayaa

 gauratlab he ki sijisti act ke section 2(17) ke tahat yadi dharm se jude trust aise kisi kaam kaa sahaara lete hai jahaan kisi vastu athwa seva ke liye paisa liya jaataa he to use kaarobaar kii shrenee ne rakhaa jayega or usapar 18 fisadi kii dar se jiesti vasula jayega
